YES

********************************************************************************
Proof Outline:

Remains to prove termination of a 7-rules system (7 strict rules).
Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
Remains to prove termination of a 21-rules system (14 strict rules).
Removing 13 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 8-rules system (1 strict rule).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 161-rules system (5 strict rules).
Removing 17 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 144-rules system (5 strict rules).
Removing 15 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 129-rules system (5 strict rules).
Applying sparse untiling TROCU(2) after reversal [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 127-rules system (3 strict rules).
Removing 22 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 105-rules system (3 strict rules).
Removing 1 rule by a matrix interpretation of dimension 4 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 104-rules system (3 strict rules).
Removing 1 rule by a matrix interpretation of dimension 4 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 103-rules system (3 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 1562-rules system (15 strict rules).
Removing 188 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 1374-rules system (15 strict rules).
Removing 88 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 1286-rules system (15 strict rules).
Applying sparse untiling TROCU(2) after reversal [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 1249-rules system (10 strict rules).
Removing 657 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 592-rules system (0 strict rules).
QED

Proof:

After renaming modulo the bijection { b ↦ 0, a ↦ 1, c ↦ 2, d ↦ 3 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 7-rules system (7 strict rules)
{ 0 1 1 ⟶ 1 0 2 ,
  2 1 ⟶ 1 2 ,
  2 0 ⟶ 0 1 ,
  1 1 0 ⟶ 3 0 1 ,
  1 3 ⟶ 3 1 ,
  0 3 ⟶ 1 0 ,
  1 1 ⟶ 1 0 1 }

Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
  Here, ↑ marks so-called defined symbols.
After renaming modulo the bijection { (0,↑) ↦ 0, (1,↓) ↦ 1, (1,↑) ↦ 2, (0,↓) ↦ 3, (2,↓) ↦ 4, (2,↑) ↦ 5, (3,↓) ↦ 6 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 21-rules system (14 strict rules)
{ 0 1 1 ⟶ 2 3 4 ,
  0 1 1 ⟶ 0 4 ,
  0 1 1 ⟶ 5 ,
  5 1 ⟶ 2 4 ,
  5 1 ⟶ 5 ,
  5 3 ⟶ 0 1 ,
  5 3 ⟶ 2 ,
  2 1 3 ⟶ 0 1 ,
  2 1 3 ⟶ 2 ,
  2 6 ⟶ 2 ,
  0 6 ⟶ 2 3 ,
  0 6 ⟶ 0 ,
  2 1 ⟶ 2 3 1 ,
  2 1 ⟶ 0 1 ,
  3 1 1 →= 1 3 4 ,
  4 1 →= 1 4 ,
  4 3 →= 3 1 ,
  1 1 3 →= 6 3 1 ,
  1 6 →= 6 1 ,
  3 6 →= 1 3 ,
  1 1 →= 1 3 1 }
